id="id_5322683f19c861e03491888"
class="text_exposed_root"><span
data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"
class="userContent">Edgar
and
Monique&#039;s
letter
to
SeaWorld!
<i
class="_4-k1
img
sp_8k12r1
sx_b17b34"></i><br
/>
<br
/>
To
Jim
Atchison
and
SeaWorld,
<br
/>
<br
/>
It
has
just
been
brought
to
my
attention
(from
many
concerned
fans
writing
into
our
web
site)
that
one
of
my
songs
&quot;Free
Ride&quot;
is
being
used
without
my
knowledge
or
consent
in
a
video
called
&quot;Shamu
Rocks.”

My
wife
Monique
and
I
share
a
deep
love
and
respect
for
all
animals,
and
are
active
in
rescue
and
care
issues.
<br
/>
<br
/>
The
id<span
class="text_exposed_hide">...</span><span
class="text_exposed_show">ea
of
these
beautiful,
and
intelligent
mammals
being
confined
to
a
small
tank,
held
in
captivity,
and
subjected
to
whatever
measures
necessary
to
force
them
to
perform
these
&quot;so
called&quot;
tricks
fills
our
hearts
with
anguish,
shame,
and
sorrow.
The
idea
behind
the
song
&quot;Free
Ride&quot;
is
freedom,
which
is
exactly
that
of
which
these
noble
and
sensitive
creatures
are
being
deprived.
<br
/>
<br
/>
I
respectfully
ask
that
you
immediately
stop
using
&quot;Free
Ride&quot;
in
this
video
or
any
similar
connection,
as
it
subverts
the
meaning
and
intention
of
the
song,
and
makes
it
appear
that
I
personally
approve
and
condone
such
activity.
<br
/>
<br
/>
Thank
you
in
advance
for
your
attention,
compliance,
and
understanding
this
resenting
and
more
compassionate
point
of
view.
<br
/>
<br
/>
Best
regards,
<br
/>
<br
/>
Edgar
and
Monique
Winter</span></span><span

40th

/>
<br
/>
Hi
Derek,<br
/>





So
glad
to
hear
you
are
coming
out
to
see
us
for
the
3rd
time
since
I
played
with
Ringo,
and
are
looking
forward
to
&quot;Free
Ride&quot;
and
&quot;Frankenstein&quot;.
Both
those
songs
were
originally
recorded
on
the
album
&quot;They
Only
Come<span
class="text_exposed_hide">...</span><span
class="text_exposed_show">
Out
At
Night&quot;,
which
was
released
in
1973.
<br
/>





This,
being
2013,
makes
it
the
fortieth
anniversary.
So,
we
have
decided
to
make
this
year
The
40eth
Anniversary
&quot;They
Only
Come
Out
At
Night&quot;
Tour!<br
/>





Since
you
have
seen
us
several
times
lately,
I
thought

might
like
to
know
this
will
be
a
different
show.
We
will
be
celebrating
by
playing
many
of
the
other
songs
from
that
album,
as
well
as
your
favorites,
&quot;Free
Ride&quot;
and
&quot;Frankenstein&quot;.<br
/>





Look
forward
to

at

festival!
All

to
-\-\-\-\
<br
/>

The
Winters<br
